 kendriya rigerv bank of india kaa sabase pramukh kaam desh main nai-puraani karency kaa sanchaar karnaa he
 It involves the distribution of new currency and new coins throughout the country, recycling old currency and keeping the excessive cash collected in all banks
 in sabhi kaam ko karne ke liye rigerv bank ke paas deshbhar main kai khajaana bananaa padataa he jise vah karency chest kahata he
 The treasury of this currency chest or Kuber is made in many places across the country, so that the currency distribution work of the Reserve Bank can be done easily
 karency chest kaa kaamadeshbhar main karency ke sanchaar ko banaae rakhane ke liye maujuuda samay main rigerv bank ke paas lagbhag 4211 karency chest hai
 In addition, it has 3990 depots for handling coins
 ye chest deshbhar main faile hue hai kyonki sanchaar ke saath-saath in khajaanon main kisi bhi saamaanya bank main jamaa karaae gaye rupayon (cash rigerv reshio) ko bhi rakhaa jaataa he
 These currency chests are playing an important role as soon as the demonetisation process starts
 sarkari prem main nai karency kii printig hone ke baad use sidhe deshbhar main faile in karency chest main pahunchaa diya jaataa he
 This map given by the Reserve Bank shows where in the country currency chests are present
 karency chest main partnerakarency chest ko deshbhar main sthapit karne ke liye rigerv bank pramukh sarkari bank state bank of india kaa sahyog letaa he
 Apart from this, 6 associate banks, all nationalized banks, a few selected private sector banks, 1 foreign bank, 1 cooperative bank and Grameen bank are also included in this work
 is kaam ko karne ke rigerv bank apane deshbhar main faile 18 branch yaa ishu offis ke jariye karata he
 How to get the currency in the chest After printing the currency in 4 government presses of the country, it is delivered directly to the 18 issue office of the Reserve Bank
 in offis tak nai karency ko pahunchane ke liye railway, air force ke maal vaahak vimaan or rajya police kii madad lee jaati he
 For container traffic in cities, large container vehicles are usually hired from the private sector for large currency movements
 is puri prakriya kii puri gopniyata rakhi jaati he or desh ke kuch samvedansheel ilaakon main suraksha ke liye sena kii madad bhi lee jaati he
 The currency is then transported to the currency chests run by other banks under the supervision of the Reserve Bank
 atm or bank shakhaon ko miltaa he rupyarijrv bank ke is vishaal network se karency ko bankig vyavastha main daalaa jaataa he
 The main work in this is the supply of money for day-to-day work in all the branches of the bank, along with the work of depositing money in the atms of all banks across the country
